1. Overview 
 
The aim of this document is recalculate the existin g south TES platform structure for supporting TES 
pipings in the central plant of Solana Generation S tation, because of there are modifications in some 
pipings routes. 
 
2. Description 
 
There are three TES platform structures on the cent ral plant as steel frame structures.The TES platfor m 
descrited in this document is the south one. The lo cations of these structures are shown in the image 
below:

- Plates and bars according to specification: 4521-ESP-ANC-00-50-3200

5.3 Loads 
 
The loads included in the structure are the same than indicated in document 4521-CAL-AGE-58-54-2001, 
except pipes loads. The old pipe loads have been eliminated. New pipes loads and piping routes that they 
haven’t been modificated, have been included again, for that, approximate supports have been modeled in 
the calculation model. 
 
In addition, the live loads of heat exchanger has been eliminated due to these equipments are unused. 
 
The summary of the loads considered are shown below according to the loads added to calculation sofwar e 
Metal 3D 2014.p. 
 
LoadCase Name Description 
DL Selfweight 
DL 1 Dead Load s 
LL 1 Live Load: Catwalks 
LL 3 (Pipes_OPE) Live Load: Pipes 
LL 3 (Standby HE_OPE) Live Load: Standby Heat Exchanger 
LL 3 (Electric HE_OPE) Live Load: Electric Heater 
LL 4 (+) Temperature + 
LL 4 ( -) Temperature - 
LL 2 (1) Live Load: Standby H eat Exchanger 
LL 2 (2) Live Load: Standby Heat Exchanger 
W 1 (+X) Wind in Equipment and Structure 
W 1 ( -Y) Wind in Equipment and Structure 
W-Suction Wind of Suction in platform of Structure

5.4 Design process 
 
Determination of calculation efforts and dimensioning of steel frame TES platform structure are done with the 
help of software Metal 3D 2014.p. 
 
Structures are designed according to the following maximum drifts: 
 
• Deflection: 1/360 of the span for floors 
 1/240 for roof members 
• Maximun drift for structures without bracings: Hei ght/300 
• Maximun drift for structures with bracings: Height /600 
 
6. Solutions 
 
As a start, an identical calculation model to the a s-built drawings has been used. They are indicated in Annex 
E. 
 
When all loads have been introduced and the model h as been calculated, it has been found that some bea ms 
failed. 
The main problems are the loads which produce torsi on in the beams. The W profiles don’t have adequate 
behaviour with these loads and they can’t resist them. 
 
Therefore, they are shown two solucions that they are described below: 
 
1º Solution: Acting on the profiles of the structure 
 
The TES structure shall be reinforced with some lat eral plates which turn W profile into a closed prof ile. They 
have a good behaviour to torsion loads. And some di agonals WT profiles to avoid rotation of the beams due 
to some of them have pinned connections. 
 
It can be seen in drawing 4521-PLN-AGE-75-54-0005.

2a Solution: Acting on the pipings supports 
 
Acting on the piping support for eliminating torsio n loads and profiles of TES structure don’t have to be 
reinforced in several points. 
 
The old piping supports shall be changed and it sha ll be designed new supports which don’t transmit to rsion 
loads to existings beams.
